And one of the biggest changes that we can see nowadays is how oblivious we , humans , are to everything that surrounds us .
We go through our daily lives lost in our minds , thinking about expenses and personal issues , so we do n't take notice of what surrounds us .
We do n't notice other people , and we do n't communicate with each other .
Lost in our minds , in our cellphones , and in our earphones .
And this is a consequence of the bad use that we have given and continue to give to technology , which fifty years from now will lead to another big change .
It 's like a vicious cycle .
Fifty years from now , people wo n't know how to talk to each other .
We will lose our social abilities .
INTRODUCTION
The purpose of this report is to explain the most important aspects of the environment in my city .
BACKGROUND
Treviso is situated in the north of Italy and it was ruined during World War II .
No changes were provided to correct .
After being rapidly rebuilt and renovated , Treviso has become a modern city .
It is easy to reach by train , rail , and air ; there has been an increase in the population thanks to the growth of industry , and all these factors have determined the enhancement of problems concerning the environment .
DEVELOPMENTS
People interviewed at the front door of the main public building , such as Town Hall , schools , etc. , have stated that they feel , on average , happy about how the council has dealt with problems involved with the new development of the town , in particular regarding the following subjects :
- Air , light , and noise pollution : about 80 % of citizens declared that they feel very satisfied with the efforts to address these problems , due to the fact that cars are not allowed to transit in the city centre ; public lights are powered by solar panels , and moreover , the Mayor has signed an agreement with the Union of builders that obliges them to create public parks in every area with 1000 people .
Recycling : all families are provided with three litter bins in which they have to recycle rubbish , and at school , children are concerned about the subject from primary school onwards .
CONCLUSION
Treviso can offer a high standard of life quality and people are aware that the result of this aim is something to be achieved together .
A historical place in Sweden , I would say , is the royal castle .
It 's located in the capital of Sweden , Stockholm .
It 's big , beautiful , and contains a lot of history .
The royal castle was rebuilt in 1697 after a fire .
It was n't in use until 1754 and it was n't finished until 1770 .
Since then , not much has been rebuilt .
On the inside , there have been some changes and modernizations to fit the royal family , and some painting on the facade on the outside .
Some museums have been added , and the royal castle is now a very popular tourist attraction .
I have never personally been there , but it would be interesting to go sometime .
An invention of the 20th century that I feel has significantly changed people 's lives is the introduction of bank cash machines or automatic teller machines .
I can not comprehend how difficult it would be without having convenient access to money in emergencies or cases when money is needed .
It is also a convenience that helps to save time , which is very important to working men and women of the late 1900s .
This machinery also permits you to do your banking when you wish , rather than during the assigned banking hours .
People may argue that ATM machines will take away employment in banks , but we must also focus on the positive aspects .
ATM machines appear in all areas of the world .
In the United States , for example , you can find machines in stores , movie theaters , parking lots at shopping malls , and at banks .
In many situations , I have either forgotten my wallet or not had enough money at the grocery store .
This is when I really appreciate having my ATM card .
Another advantage of the card is that it eliminates the danger of having large quantities of cash in your home or wallet .
This attracts robbers and can promote danger .
All in all , I feel that ATM cards are an excellent invention . The convenience has proved itself in many circumstances and I do not know what I would do without my card . The development of computerized technology has enhanced our environment , providing convenience and time-saving activities which reduce the stress of our everyday life .
The Amazon lava lizards are pretty hard to see .
When you saw one , it probably already saw you .
I noticed in the field that the big males are more conspicuous than the juveniles , the immature males , and the females .
The adult males seemed to be in the same place all the time .
However , I ca n't confirm that those were the same males in the same places .
The smaller individuals had a tendency to run away quickly when they noticed someone coming .
Also , they commonly return to the same place just after they flee .
The lizards can stand still for a long time with few movements , usually of their head .
The big ones showed more communicative displays , like headbobs and push-ups .
The boardwalk was the only point where I saw more than one animal that could interact with each other .
In other places , when there is more than one animal , they are away from one another and do n't interact .
The animals which use the boardwalk were most exposed than the animals at the other points .
The animals that I observed among the vegetation were usually sheltered either by dense shrubs or bush vegetation , or on a bromeliad leaf that had spikes on the edge .
The distance to cause them to flee in these animals was larger than in the boardwalk lizards .

Using the Global Positioning System , GPS , is popular in the modern world , although GPS does not work that well in areas where the GPS signal is interfered with .
Consequently , indoor navigation with GPS is not that good .
This paper aims to propose an alternative method to GPS for use in indoor environments .
The methods developed in this paper use only the position of the Wireless Access Points ( WAPs ) and the signal strength ( RSSI ) recorded by the user in order to calculate the position of the device .
Since today 's computers and cellphones contain all the required hardware , a future adoption of these methods would not only be easy but also cost-effective .
One of the methods proposed in this paper usually gives the user a position that is about five meters off .
Therefore , this method can not be used when a more precise estimation is needed .
However , a weighted average of these three methods , together with different similar methods , might enhance the accuracy .

The justifications behind it are :
The advanced technology reduces the costs of manufacturing and maintaining an automobile to a very affordable level .
2 .

The more comfortable way is to have a private car with which it is possible to take the highway and then head in the direction of the city centre .
My home is close to the central rail station and the most important bus stops in the metropolitan area .
As a second option , there is a railway service from the airport to a secondary rail station .
Here you have to get off and then take bus number 25 , with which it is possible to arrive in the centre of the city , from where I can reach my home on foot .
Another possible option is to use a taxi service , but in this case , the cost of the journey is the most expensive of all .
The two best choices to return home from the airport are to use a private car or to use the railway airport service , which offers a very cheap service . I spend a bit more time and money , but the journey is nice and comfortable , similar to the same trip in a private car .

The pie chart depicts the different proportions of fuel types that generate energy in Florida in 2007 compared with the forecast for 2017 .
Overall , it is clear that natural gas is the main energy generator for both years , while renewables and oil come at the bottom of the list .
For example , the energy generated by natural gas increased from 38.8 % in 2007 to 54.4 % in 2017 .
Next comes the energy production by coal , which accounts for 29.3 % of the energy market in 2007 , followed by a drop of 5.6 % in the forecasted year of 2017 .
As for Nuclear , although it represents the third energy generator in Florida for both the compared years , the trend here is upwards , reaching 15.9 % in the estimated period .
In contrast , there is a significant drop in energy production for both oil and other sources over the two separate years , from 6.7 % to 1.1 % for the former and from 11.1 % to 3.4 % for the latter .
As for renewables , the decrease in fuel generated over the period is less dramatic .

There are many problems facing both road and rail transport in the UK .
The most talked-about issues concerning roads are probably congestion and safety .
Congestion is most apparent around the major conurbations such as London , Greater Manchester , and Birmingham .
The simple way to solve this problem would be to either build more roads or make the present ones larger is not needed , The simple way to solve this problem would be to either build more roads or to make the present ones larger .
However , as seen in recent events , for example Newbury , this has been met with strong opposition from environmental groups and local residents .
Another way to reduce congestion , especially in the large cities , could be to persuade people not to use their vehicles at all .
Introducing schemes such as the 'park-and-ride ' scheme and encouraging people to use bicycles would certainly reduce the number of cars on the road .
Safety is often talked about as a priority factor regarding roads .
Too many accidents occur because of dangerous driving on busy roads .
There are several ways to combat this problem .
Although the legal limit for drinking while driving has just been increased , lowering the limit by several units would deter many people from using their own vehicles and instead encourage them to use public transport .
Increasing the amount of law enforcement could also be effective , giving the police more authority to make arrests and increasing the number of speed cameras , as well as possibly imposing larger fines .
Cutting down on the national speed limit may also encourage drivers to take more care .
The condition of roads is often a local issue rather than of national concern .
It is therefore up to the local council to maintain its roads better , especially in winter .
This may require the local council to obtain more money from the government .
Safety is much less of a factor in rail transport .
Here , the major talking point is efficiency .
It is often noted that trains are delayed and rarely run on time .
Because of this inefficiency , many of rail 's customers are turning to other forms of transport , cars mostly , but for long-distance journeys , flying is an increasingly attractive option .
A large amount of blame for this inefficiency goes to the actual trains , which are in most cases out of date and slower than modern ones , such as the French TGV or the Japanese 'bullet ' train .
The train tracks can also be blamed , as they are often in a state of disrepair and this inevitably delays trains .
It is hoped that the recent privatisation of British Rail will bring in more up-to-date trains and increase the overall efficiency of travelling by train in a bid to attract many more customers .

Because it is a controversial topic , there are arguments for and against it .
Depending on the point of view that each person might take , the argument they will give will vary .
It is very likely that animals in zoos suffer from not being in their natural habitat , being stared at almost all the time , not having the space they require to live comfortably , and the natural peace they need to live .
Furthermore , it is also , but not only , important to say that the fact that its animals live in groups , and in contrast , in zoos , their number is limited to a few of them .
Nevertheless , it is very useful for society and especially for children to have the possibility of going to and experiencing a visit to a zoo .

All in all , it would be difficult to find a fair solution , or almost impossible to provide one that would deal with both sides of the topic in question .
In my personal opinion , I believe that safari parks would be a solution that strikes a balance between these opposing views ; they would provide a better quality of life for animals and would also be educational .
What is the European Union ?
It seems to have two distinct forms , of which one seems to worry the British public most : Political Union , followed by Economic and Monetary Union .
In fact , these issues have become so heated in Great Britain at present that they have led to many disputes within the present government .
They also appear to be one of the major reasons for Mrs. Thatcher 's resignation .
In losing her , have we not already lost part of our sovereignty ?
Europe is forcing change upon us as we have been attempting to stand back , " not letting socialism in by the back door " , instead of playing an important role in positively affecting the decision-making processes in the European Community .
Great Britain can not afford to play a minor role in a two-speed Europe , especially in the time of recession at present , and this has manifested itself in the top governmental disputes .
So , a loss of sovereignty seems inevitable , whether we like it or not .
On a monetary and economic union , I do n't feel that we have much to lose ; in fact , on the contrary , I think that we would benefit enormously , especially in the light of 1992 .
If only the issue were presented in a more positive light , perhaps with some modifications , I am sure that the British public would give its agreement .
After all , how long has it been since we lost our sovereignty to the follies of the international Stock Exchanges of New York , Tokyo , and Frankfurt ?
Will losing our sovereignty to Brussels or the Bundesbank make a big difference ?

I therefore see this European unity as a natural process in world development , something which should be made easier rather than hindered .

Yes , we have a Queen , and what would happen to her - would she be forced to abdicate and be succeeded by King Jacques Delors ?
This is a very typical , misinformed , and ignorant statement posed by certain British " patriots " .
There are five other monarchs in the European Community and their statuses , to a great extent , will not be greatly affected by any such union .
But there is a true cause for concern about Brussels ' bureaucracy , which rightly worries the British public .
This situation must be changed to rid the Council of its secrecy and to transfer more power to the European Parliament for a more democratic system .
This will mean that everyone will have a fair say in what goes on - something which must be guaranteed for such independent thinkers as the Britons themselves .

If properly carried out , this would enable us to keep our cultural identity , the ultimate element of our sovereignty .
Dementia is a kind of disease common in the elderly population .
And it is difficult for humans to cure it , so robotics are used to help them .
For this case , at this monument , research reported that :
Social commitment robots are designed to promote therapeutic interactions with humans through various interactive methods , such as conversation , emotional support , and assistance with daily tasks . However , based on the input given , a possible corrected and completed sentence could be : Social commitment robots are designed to promote therapeutic interactions through various interactive methods .
Communication and social interaction .
The therapeutic use of robots attempts to
reach out to people affected by dementia and may provide an alternative mode of communication
engagement with this population
( Mordoch et al. , 2013 , p. 15 )
Consequently , these robotics offer benefits to patients who are associated with personal interactions , enabling them to feel pleased and relaxed .
Especially in Japan , people are keen on using robots to care for the aging population . The reason for this is that homes or hospitals can not allow animal-assisted therapy to enter .
Unlike Japan , in North America , people prefer to use animal-assisted therapy , but the use of robotics is less than that of animals .

Colombia 's army is a good example compared to other armies in Latin America and even other armies around the world .
Even so , many Colombians do not know that the hard work of their soldiers day by day must be done for the sole purpose of protecting our lives and guaranteeing democracy for all of us .
Therefore , it is necessary to know why the Colombian army has this distinction .
First , the military forces of Colombia have 438,700 effectives , being the largest army in Latin America , followed by Brazil .
On the other hand , the Colombian army is regarded as one of the best armies in the world due to its internal conflict , which keeps the soldiers in action and constant training . Even in Colombia , they train other Latin American armies from Africa and the Middle East because of the anti-terrorist war that the Colombian armed forces have developed for 40 years , and as a result , they have been strengthened in a masterly manner , with their preparation , intelligence , and modern tactical aids .
Second , it is necessary to highlight some of the work performed by our army in the anti-terrorism struggle , such as : foiling terrorist attacks , neutralizing explosive devices left in urban and rural areas , preventing the recruitment of children , organizing medical brigades to help farmers , and most importantly , offering their lives if necessary to protect each and every one of us , even if they do not know us .
Finally , I can say that the hard work and the good image that the Colombian army has just reflect our wish to live in peace .
Likewise , all the Colombian people want to reach their dreams in a peaceful way , without weapons or fights between brothers , and so , show the world that the Colombian people are brave enough to fight for peace .

Scientists around the world are investigating genetic manipulation for a wide variety of beneficial purposes .
Genetic engineering is , however , a very raw issue , and there is a lot of resistance to this work , and certainly to the suggestions of using it on humans .
The trouble is that although a scientist may think he knows a lot about a particular area of study , and indeed he may , there is still so much that we do not know about areas of study like genetics that there is a great fear of the unexpected . Corrected sentence : The trouble is that although a scientist may think he knows a lot about a particular area of study , and indeed he may , there is still so much that we do not know about areas of study like genetics , that there is a great fear of the unexpected . becomes The trouble is that although a scientist may think he knows a lot about a particular area of study , and indeed he may , there is still so much that we do not know about areas of study like genetics , which creates a great fear of the unexpected . Result : The trouble is that although a scientist may think he knows a lot about a particular area of study , and indeed he may , there is still so much that we do not know about areas of study like genetics , which creates a great fear of the unexpected .
And indeed , this fear is justified .
When we consider the horrific effects of a nuclear holocaust , I am sure there are many who wish it had never been invented .
But are we right to blame the scientists who first started the research and who had no idea it would be used as a weapon .
We can argue that surely the scientist must have the greatest realization of the uses of the discovery , good or bad , since he is the expert on the subject .
But are we right to blame him ?
Let us assume that he has discovered a cure for cancer as a result of genetic engineering .
It is against human nature to stop at this stage and ask , " Should I introduce what could be the greatest medical discovery of our lifetime when I am not 100 % sure of the consequences ? "
Can we expect a scientist to bear this additional burden for the whole world ?
In truth , no , it is unreasonable .
Genetic engineering is developing rapidly and has already been used extensively in plants and bacteria , notably for the production of resistant strains of plants and in the production of human insulin .
The natural step forward now is to apply this knowledge to treat common genetic disorders like Down syndrome .
There is a lot of resistance to this and fears that we may manufacture mutants or that somebody may produce an army of superhuman clones . becomes There is a lot of resistance to this , and there are fears that we may manufacture mutants or that somebody may produce an army of superhuman clones .
Some of these may seem a little far-fetched , but it is conceivable that in 100 years ' time , we may be able to decide the characteristics of our child , whether he is a great piano player or a sportsman .
It does not seem morally right to make these decisions , and certainly for anyone who is religious , it would be seen as interfering in the ways of God , something to be avoided at all costs .
A great scientist can not see into the future .
He can not gauge the moral repercussions of his discovery nor the long-term effect it is going to have on the world .
If he is doing research for what he considers to be a good cause , who are we to criticise him when we know far less about it ?
Provided a scientist 's work has been published and is public , I feel it is unjust to hold him responsible for what the world will make of his work .
To avoid continually writing he/she , his/her , the scientist in this essay has been referred to as he .
I hope no offence is taken at this .
Dear Sir/Madam ,
I am writing in response to the invitation to share my experience of making a hard decision that appeared in the July issue of your English-language magazine .
As a nineteen-year-old student , I have gained familiarity with this topic by deciding which course of studies I was going to choose .
First of all , I strongly believe that making choices is always risky , as people do not know what the exact result will be .
Like most adolescents , I was at a total loss when the time for deciding what I wanted to be in the future came .
In despair , I applied for two courses of study that did not resemble each other at all , which made the moment of choosing a lot harder .
Knowing that not only was this choice a fundamental decision , but it was also one that would influence the rest of my adulthood , I appealed for help in deciding what I should focus on at the moment of making my decision .
As time passed by , I had to attend more and more classes .
I could not cope with such a busy timetable and consequently I was exhausted and stressed .
A decision had to be made before I dropped out of both courses of study .
I bore in mind the pieces of advice I was given and chose what made me happy , despite not having the approval of some of my relatives .
I am convinced that stark choices are unavoidable , but in order to not regret the consequences they might have , either positive or negative , people should choose what makes them happier .
However , I have not given for granted that my decision will not make me regret .
If this were the case , I know that I am always on time to start again .
For the aforementioned reasons , I think choices have to be carefully considered before being made .
Even though this does not assure the results .
I look forward to following subsequent articles on related issues .
Yours faithfully
Vilma Rossi
There are many standards by which success and hard work have been measured and rewarded in the past .
In earlier times , people had a lifestyle of fending for themselves .
They were not afforded the many luxuries that have become commonplace in our present-day society .
Because of the differences in personalities and ambition , I feel it is vital that in today 's society men and women should be financially rewarded for their individual efforts .
In a society , each person has the same basic needs for survival .
Long ago , the quest for fulfillment of these needs took up the majority of each person 's day .
In order to feed your family , you had to plant .
In order to live , you had to build .
To have clothing , you had to do some sewing .
Each hour of every day was devoted to meeting these needs .
Even in early times , the harder you worked , the more food , shelter , or clothing you gained .
This is a very simple system of reward equaling effort .
Bringing this to a more present time , we are now reaping the benefits of advanced technology , expanding knowledge , and the modern times .
We have many machines to help us meet our food , clothing , and shelter needs with little or no effort on our part , it would appear .
Persons with great technical minds are using their talent on the job and paying someone else to do their labor .
However , just as in earlier days , the harder you work , the greater the rewards are .
Let 's imagine a society where all men and women were treated equally .
All basic survival needs ( and even wants , for that matter ) were provided , regardless of the effort put forth . I would venture to guess that we would not be as advanced a society as we are today .
Competitiveness and jealousy would set in and fights would occur .
Worst-case scenario : the world would become divided or even destroyed because someone was sitting on the sidelines and not doing their part .
We would not have the motivation to develop our talents and abilities and to use them in a way that benefits others .
Our society would become selfish and materialistic , and our culture would suffer .
It may be a pessimistic view , but I feel it 's a very real one to say that we would become lazy and stagnant people .
Life is not just about rewards .
It is about learning where you are and how you can move to the next level .
Each of us is measured daily by some scale of achievement .
Effort is vital to success ; motivation is the key to effort .
Some are content with their needs , others want more , much more !
Our system of rewards is based on money ... but is it really about money ?
I do n't think so .
It 's about meeting needs ( and even wants ! ) and how much one is willing to give for the opportunity of something better .

Once you become famous , you will probably definitely know the taste and the price of fame .
There are many people in my country who keep thinking that being a famous person , to some extent , is a blessing .
Such a person is known to most people on a national or even international scale .
Some believe that there are many advantages to being a celebrity or widely known person , though there are a number of disadvantages as well .
First of all , many local and world-known celebrities claim to have no private life .
Being famous means that probably most of your life , journalists , your neighbours , and ordinary people will be interested in your life .
Most of the time , it is impossible to avoid this kind of attention .
People are curious and they follow their favourite stars ' lives by reading magazines , watching TV or surfing the Internet .
Moreover , such yellow press columns with the title 'celebrities ' hit the sales records , giving huge benefits for the publishing companies .
Millions of people are able to buy magazines with celebrities on the covers , although some photos give the readers some 'additional ' , and not the most pleasant , details .
People are interested in almost everything : articles about break-ups , drug abuse by young celebrities , questionable relationships , or even the special ones with naked celebrity photos .
This is more than sharing some of your private life details ; most of the press people look for scandals , and their aim is to uncover the most intimate secrets .
Secondly , being successful and famous also requires that the person be good at their job .
The 'star ' is followed not only by the public eye ; he or she is also evaluated by producers and future employing companies .
There is no doubt that celebrities work hard to achieve fame , better and more desirable jobs , including superior salaries .
The majority of celebrities have personal managers , who take care of their image .
So even if you are rich and famous , it does n't always mean that you will be able to live and act as you would like to .
Fame has another side ; there are strict requirements for actors , singers , etc. , which become apparent when they sign contracts with the companies that provide their jobs .
Attending some events or parties may be a necessity and not always depend on the wishes of a celebrity .
Also , it is said that fame spoils people and they struggle with their personal problems , only it is even more difficult to help them than any ordinary people .
Sometimes there are cases when the lack of private life leads to more serious issues .
We all know that some well-known people become engaged in illegal activities , start using drugs or alcohol , and also join some mysterious religious groups .
Sometimes they even become suicidal just because they can not live under the constant pressure .
Even if being in the public eye is not always very pleasant , there are a number of advantages as to why it is worth sacrificing a little of your private life .
Going deep into the public entertainment world , which is definitely rewarding , gives you a lot of benefits .
Most celebrities do not work all their lives , although the money they gain during their careers ( sometimes it is a very short period of success ) allows them to live without any worries .
Giving away some personal life details while you are famous may bring you fortune .
For example , many celebrities sell photos of their newborn babies to magazines , as they offer enormous sums of money , in order to get a tiny glimpse into their family life .
Moreover , being a famous person means that you are able to influence other people , especially the young generation .
By setting a good example , celebrities may become idols and inspire other people to live and help others who are in need .
By donating money to charities , as well as being involved in volunteering projects , is one of the things you can do when you are wealthy and famous .
To summarise , fame comes with many disadvantages , but it also has a number of advantages .
Celebrities have different experiences .
Their lives seem to be glamorous and they look gorgeous , though you will never know what lies under the beautiful and sparkling cover .

Terrorism is the use of fear and acts of violence in order to intimidate societies or governments .
Many different types of social or political organizations might use terrorism to try to achieve their goals .
It is difficult to define terrorism .
Terrorism has no universally accepted criminal law definition at the international level .
Common definitions of terrorism refer to violent acts that are intended to create fear ( terror ) , are done for a religious , political , or ideological goal , and target civilians .
Some definitions now include acts of unlawful violence and war .
The use of similar tactics by criminal gangs is not usually called terrorism , though these same actions may be called terrorism when carried out by a politically motivated group .

Not only does public transport have a future , but it also deserves a bright one .
Despite the fact that travelling by car may be more comfortable , we all should be absolutely conscious that public transport ought to occupy a prime spot in our future mobility .
Otherwise , the future of the Earth could be put in danger .
Indeed , if we , as a civilized society , were aware of the problem of the greenhouse gases that are time and again expelled into the atmosphere , we would use public transport much more often .
In this way , air pollution would be reduced as a consequence of the use of buses , trains , or the underground , all of which are public means of transport that can avoid the massive presence of private cars in our streets and roads .
Apart from cutting down on polluting gases in the atmosphere , the safety of our roads would improve , as there would be fewer cars on the roads throughout the country .
Both effects would combine to offer a healthier environment in which our children could grow up safely .
On top of that , there is no excuse to use public transport , as it has been remarkably improved over the last few years .
Nowadays it is almost possible to access any place at any time by public transport , erasing as a result one of the main problems that public transport used to have for its potential users .
So if we are determined to preserve our beloved planet and make it a better place to live in , a definitely good start would be to leave the car in the garage and take the bus .

Genetic manipulation is an area that has caused a great deal of controversy within the scientific field with a number of advantages and disadvantages .
One of the main advantages is the ability to tailor other organisms ' genetic makeup towards human needs .
The possibilities are endless . A crop could be designed that would grow in the dry , hot conditions of many third-world countries , relieving them of their worries about starvation .
Cattle could be bred that are more efficient at converting plant energy to body mass , or even diseased cattle could be killed off by altering people 's resistance to them .
Of course , to some extent , genetic manipulation already exists .
Racehorses are bred from certain combinations of parents , and gardeners cross-breed plants to suit their individual needs .
However , there is much opposition to the process of genetic mutation .
The advantages seem very favourable and I 'm sure that a scientist would gain much credit for these .
But would he accept the blame if he caused one of the many disadvantages of genetic manipulation ?
There are many possibilities for the misuse of this process .
One is a matter of ethics and morals .
Is it right to try and change someone 's motive ?
Is it right for one man to play God ?
It is also possible that we would not be able to control the new organisms that are created by genetic engineering .
A new plant which has an increased growth rate may seem like an answer to all our problems , but what would we do if suddenly it upset the ecosystem , draining the soil of its nutrients and not allowing other plants to grow ?
In theory , a scientist should take responsibility for this , but in an area such as genetic manipulation , of which we do not know a great deal , it may not be possible to find a solution .
Another problem would be the testing process .
We are already near the stage where it is possible to test people 's genetic makeup to find the possibility of their developing certain illnesses .
Soon it may be possible for firms to employ only people with a certain expected lifespan or for insurance companies to refuse to insure certain individuals on the basis of a genetic test .

An essay .
It is widely known that the majority of teenagers are keen on video games .
Some people believe that it 's a waste of time and a bad habit too , while some others think that it 's a good way to spend your free time .
In my mind , there are pros and cons .
First of all , computer games can help you escape from your busy schedule and get some rest and relaxation after school .
Apart from that , it 's quite convenient mainly because you stay at home and have entertainment .
Also , video games are more interesting than traditional toys , so they capture teenagers ' interest .
Last but not least , some of them are educational and give you an ideal opportunity to gain knowledge .
On the other hand , there are many drawbacks .
To begin with , when you spend a lot of hours in front of the computer screen , you become addicted to it .
As a result , you do n't get together with your friends and you do n't communicate face-to-face .
In addition , a lot of video games are full of violence and teens tend to imitate them , which leads to violent and aggressive behavior .
Playing video games for hours is also very harmful to your eyes .
In conclusion , computer games are a nice way to spend your free time , but always in moderation .
I feel that the invention of the computer has significantly changed people 's lives .
This , realistically , has been a quite new invention , and in its short life span , it has been able to change the world significantly .
Not to mention how it will change people 's lifestyles in the future .
These changes , resulting from the invention of the computer , have been , I feel , both bad and good .
Technologically , computers have drastically improved people 's lives .
No longer are we in the times when people must write a paper manually , or even with a simple typewriter .
Personal computers are becoming quite common , and therefore , they are less expensive and easier to own .
Computers have also made life transpire much quicker than before .
Gone are the days when a person who wanted money from a bank had to wait until it opened .
We now have ATMs , automatic teller machines , that are able to process the same transactions as a teller would do .
It seems these days that everything is run by computers !
We are able to complete our tasks much better and more efficiently .
Basically , every facet of life has been affected by computers , bringing about positive results .
While computers have brought about improvements , in my opinion , they have also " impersonalized " the world .
Jobs are being taken away from humans who are not fast enough .
Interaction with humans in some places is extinct .
Yes , it might be more efficient to have a computer make your transaction at a bank , but I miss the human interaction between people .
In addition , it is also very dangerous to place all of one 's trust in a machine . becomes In addition , it is also very dangerous to place all one 's trust in a machine .
It is a common fact that machines do fail .
Sure , a car with a computer that tells the driver when an oncoming obstacle is approaching is safe , but what happens when the driver relies too much on the computer and not enough on their own brain ?
People soon stop thinking and allow machines to do the work for them .
I feel uneasy when our society relies so heavily on a bunch of wires .
Computers are not able to express and truly feel emotions , and therefore are incapable , in some instances , of functioning .
With the invention of the computer , many changes have come , from the lifestyle of the past to changes in the lifestyle of the future .
Some of these changes will save people 's lives , such as advances in medical technology and safety .
But I fear that our world will become a very impersonalized place .
I hope that we will be able to determine what improvements should be made and what should just remain slow .

The Single European Act , signed in February 1986 by the Heads of Government of the 12 Member States of the European Community , which came into force on 1st July 1987 , aims to create a single market by the end of 1992 .
This major target is to be attained by the removal of all fiscal , technical , and physical barriers .
This means that a merchant or tradesman would be able to sell his goods in any country in the community , an individual would be able to borrow and deposit money in the banks of any member state and also work in any member state with national qualifications .
There would also be the introduction of a European passport and an integrated transportation system .
Despite the fact that the proposals put forward to amend the Treaty of Rome came from an Englishman , namely Lord Cobfield , there has been widespread dissatisfaction in Britain regarding the single market , shown by frequent discussions in Parliament and letters to leading national newspapers , whereas Jacques Delors , the president of the European Commission , described the measures adopted as a mere compromise .
In accordance with the Constitution of Britain , Parliament is the supreme law-making body in the United Kingdom .
Consequently , the emergence of another source of law , deemed to be supranational , is inevitably a problem .
One of the prerogative powers conferred upon the Crown is the right to make treaties .
However , these treaties are not directly effective on British individuals , so where a treaty contains provisions giving rights and duties to an individual , he can not place reliance upon the treaty until it is substantially incorporated into the law of the United Kingdom by an Act of Parliament .
This acts as a curb on the enforcement of European Community Law , so that to a certain extent , a degree of sovereignty is retained .
Yet , this is not as advantageous as it may at first appear , for there exists a general judicial presumption that Parliament does not intend to legislate contrary to European community law .
Personally , I think that although the integration of Britain into Europe will be beneficial in so many matters , such as freedom of transportation , movement , work , and many other realms , there are also many disadvantages in store , including the loss of sovereignty to a certain extent .
Although the British Parliament will continue to regulate the acts or omissions of individuals on a personal basis , for example in criminal law , its freedom to legislate in the domain of public law will be severely restricted .
Not only will Parliament be obliged to enforce Community law , but also any later statutes passed by the British Parliament will either be construed in the light of Community provisions or be declared invalid .
To conclude , it is feasible to imply that the sovereignty of Britain will be impaired in many ways , although only within the sphere of Community Law that prevails over national law .
In other senses , the sovereignty of Britain will be safeguarded , for Parliament will still reign supreme within the United Kingdom .
The turn of the century has brought with it many changes that have greatly altered lives throughout the globe .
Each decade in itself has introduced a new " fad " or discovery that has become fixed in our minds as " typical " of the era .
The " Roaring Twenties , " for example , was marked by flapper skirts and the invention of the automobile .
A very capricious decade , it can be contrasted with the years of hunger and unemployment that marked the " Great Depression " of the 1930s .
How could we ever forget the " Fabulous Fifties " or the hippie decades of the 60 's and 70 's ?
For change is inevitable , and as difficult as it may be to pinpoint any one accomplishment that has taken place over the last 100 years as the most remarkable , there is one aspect of the 20th Century that will remain with me forever .
So as we embark on the year 2000 , I think it is only fair to call the 20th century , " The Century of Democracy . "
Perhaps it is because today is November 4th , the day after the U.S. elections .
Perhaps it is because the former superpower , the Soviet Union , is now making its transition into a democracy .
Perhaps it is because I am thousands of miles from my home , but I 'm feeling very patriotic these days .
No , I 'm not engulfed in the typical ethnocentric idealism of a citizen of the United States .
Rather , I 'm feeling patriotic because I can look around the world today and see that it is becoming a better place to live in for people of all nations .
In the past 2 years alone , we have seen people all over the world finally take a stand for what they believe in .
Not too long ago , I remember the democratic demonstrations that caused the people of East and West Germany to unite as one democratic nation .
At the World Expo in Sevilla , not a month ago , I bought a chunk of what was once the Berlin Wall - the Wall that was a symbol to many of the harsh realities of the Cold War .
That wall is gone forever and I feel lucky to be among the many who could witness its fall .
The Soviet Union , as well , is going through its own transition to democracy .
The many unhappy people of this troubled nation finally took it upon themselves to rid their nation of its communist government .
The superpower among superpowers that , to me , had long been the example of Marxism , is now following in the footsteps of the rest of the world .
With the end of the Cold War , there have been more peaceful relations throughout the world .
The idea of a nuclear war is practically nonexistent today .
Arms sales have gone down so that nations can spend this money in more worthwhile areas .
In conclusion , as the turn of the century slowly approaches , I look back with a feeling of accomplishment as well as anticipation for what lies ahead .
As a world comprising many scattered nations , conflict is inevitable .
However , if we all have one bond - democracy - then maybe together , we can learn to understand one another and work towards a happier world for all .

Secondly , we should consider two main options : going abroad or staying around our home .
This could be the first question that we wonder about before going on holiday .
Nowadays , due to globalization and the increased number of flights around the world , we can find a wide range of webpages where flight companies offer their services at incredibly low prices .
Because of these low prices , many people decide to go abroad instead of travelling near their home .
Of course , in order to prepare for a good trip , you must also consider the accommodation , the food , etc. , and , depending on the place you choose , you will spend more or less money .
Another point to consider should be the environment . If you go abroad , you can visit the most well-known typical monuments and historical natural places around the world . If you stay in your country , although it is sure you can see a lot of places , the things to see are limited .
In conclusion , I think one person must consider several points when planning a holiday trip and it depends on the person 's knowledge about where to go and how , to determine if one trip could be cheaper or more expensive .

The European Community is a grouping of 12 sovereign European States whose intention is to develop closer economic and political cooperation .
Its intention is to encourage greater freedom of movement of goods and also of services , capital , and the workforce .
The competition for trade in modern times is so great that Britain has no choice but to join Europe in order to increase the market for its goods .
Britain has been recognised as having a particular skill in the areas of banking and insurance . ( No changes needed , however I will make sure it is perfect ) Britain has been recognised as having a specific skill in the areas of banking and insurance .
The European market will give us the opportunity to use this skill in a far wider market .
The creation of a European commercial market will also benefit the consumer , since a harmonization of standards is also in the process of being introduced , hopefully to the highest common denominator .
The European Union does not serve only as a useful trade association , however , because environmental problems can be tackled more effectively if the European community confronts such problems together .
Cooperation between the communities and police forces will assist in overcoming the problems of drug-smuggling and terrorism .
The common defence policy of such a large area of Europe would also be beneficial and possibly less costly if the member states pooled their resources . ( No changes needed , but I 'll make sure ) The common defence policy of such a large area of Europe would also be beneficial and possibly less costly if the member states pooled their resources .
However , some loss of national sovereignty will inevitably occur .
The Single European Act was designed to speed up the decision-making of certain institutions .
The act meant that member governments had to be committed to greater co-operation and joint action in the areas of foreign , social and environmental policy , thus leaving less room for differences of opinion among the members .
The decisions of the European Court of Justice already take precedence over national law , which can be seen as a major infringement on our national sovereignty .
More participation in the election of members of the European Parliament would help to elect those best able to promote British interests in Europe .
The question is how much sovereignty Britain is prepared to lose and whether the benefits of belonging to a single Europe outweigh the disadvantages .
A certain loss of sovereignty has already been felt and in the next few years this will increase even further .
As far as the immediate future is concerned , a certain loss of sovereignty is the price we have to pay for material progress .
In most of the earlier studies , the effect of either ocean acidification or warming has been investigated at one time .
However , in nature , these stressors affect the organism combinedly , and the effect could be more than the effect of a single stressor .

On the other hand , everyone is more or less aware that airline companies have a great impact on air pollution .

We must also take into consideration the fact that the car industry has developed lots of new vehicles .
There are now available new models , for example , electric cars , that are environmentally friendly ; they are not so expensive , so everyone can buy one of them .
In conclusion , I strongly believe that there is no future for public transport and that travelling by car will be day by day faster , cheaper , and even environmentally less hazardous .

" Take me to the airport " repeated in his mind , but no , that was too crazy .

He felt the guilt of leaving in the very second he grabbed the cab door .

No .
It was because of her daughter ?
No .
It was because of his poorly paid job .
No .
It was because he did not have the courage , and it was selfish and incorrect .
But the question rounding his mind was : " Does that really matter ? " .
Michael closed the door and knew at that moment that he had made a mistake .

SOCIAL NETWORKS
If you want to talk with your friends , share photos , or post anything you want , you have so many opportunities to do that : social sites .
Nowadays , people use the Internet to do anything - from taking information to sharing photos , uploading videos and other useful things .
So , social networks are very widespread now on the internet .
The most popular social networks are Facebook , Twitter , Yahoo , Flickr , WhatsApp , Tumblr , Ask.fm , and so on .
Let 's take Facebook as an example .
Facebook is the biggest and the most used social network .
It has more than 1 billion users .
You can use a Facebook account for texting your friends , keeping in touch with them , sharing your own experiences , receiving notifications , uploading photos and videos , and , of course , seeing what your friends post .
You can also see their opinion and what 's new in politics , business , and entertainment .
You can promote your own business , so your products and services can find their target more easily .
Facebook has a lot of benefits , but at the same time , it can be very dangerous .
There are so many people on the internet who pretend they are someone else .
Now , let me tell you my story on Facebook .
When I was 11 years old , I created my first Facebook account .
I was so excited about it !
I felt like I had just discovered the technology .
I started to post photos of myself , share videos , update my status , and meet new people .
Then , I was thinking that it 's " cooler " to write on Facebook that I live in the Netherlands and work at Jack Daniel 's .
I remember that I used to answer everybody , no matter who they were .
I talked with Romanian , Indian English , Arab , and other strangers .
I did n't realise I was in danger .
Two years later , when I was 13 years old , I started to realise that my old photos , videos , and status were completely stupid , and I decided to delete them all !
I have also changed my workplace and my country , and I deleted the unknown people from my " friends list " , but I made a really big mistake : I made my phone number public !
One week later , after making my phone number public , I was called by a lot of strangers and some of them were using a private number .
I really did n't like it !
Now , I 'm 15 years old and I think I 'm mature enough to use Facebook . I have learned a lot from the big mistakes I made on Facebook until now .
I do n't accept friend requests from people I do n't know , I do n't talk to strangers , I do n't share my personal details ( especially my phone number ) , and I think twice before posting something .
I 'm thinking now : What was going through my mind when I was talking with strangers ?
Oh my God , I was in really big danger !
So , I want to give you some advice : Do n't let your kids access Facebook if they are under 13 years old because they can be very naive and psychopaths , rapists , and so on are everywhere on the Internet .
In my opinion , social networks can be useful if you know how to use them , as long as you do n't let them control you .

Wawel - The Managing Center of the old capital city .
Wawel was once one of the most important places in Central Europe for most of the interval of time in the Middle Ages .
There was a living and leading brave Polish king and leaders in a time when Poland was once one of the strongest countries in the world and the strongest in Central Europe .
The Wawel is currently ranked number one in Kraków for visitors because , apart from its brave history , we can find nice monuments , works of art , and obviously , we can get a lot of interesting information on a tour with a guide .
Apart from tourism , history is being created on Wawel recently - there we can visit a cemetery , where the most famous leaders of Poland , like Jan III Sobieski , Józef Piłsudski , or Lech Kaczyński , who was the President of Poland recently , had been laid to rest .

It was the day before yesterday , but Michael did not know this yet .
He just knew that he had to get to work on the novel , which he so desperately wanted to finish , but had not managed to complete a single chapter so far .
He placed himself in front of the oak desk , opened his silver laptop , and stared at the white , blank page of the document in front of him .
He did not know what to write , even though he knew the story , the characters , the plot , and the twists at the end .
He knew the complexity , essence , feel , and every last detail of what he wanted to create or express in his writing . or He knew the complexity , essence , feel , and every last detail of what he wanted to write about .
Suddenly , he felt his mind running in circles , spiralling into the unknown . His fingers blazed over the keyboard faster than he had ever done it before , and the words assembled , gathered , and became sentences - structured organisations of semantic meaning . And suddenly , the chapter was finished .
He had no doubt that the inspiration came from above .
He closed the writing program and when asked whether or not to save the changes , he pressed " Do n't Save " as he always did after not writing anything , and then put on his jacket to go for a walk to celebrate .
He went out the door , turned on his heel , and looked back at his computer with a strange sensation in his stomach .
Michael closed the door and knew at that moment that he had made a mistake .

However , it is still perfectly legal for a group of people to chase a fox with a pack of dogs and watch them chase the fox until it is exhausted and then get torn apart by the dogs .
This , apparently , is a sport .
The Government has made it illegal for dogs to attack badgers , while it is still legal for dogs to attack foxes .
Surely this is unfair and hypocritical of the government .
It is also illegal for two dogs to fight each other for the enjoyment of spectators .
At least if one dog fights another , the fight is , in some ways , fair .
But it is still perfectly legal for an infinite number of dogs to attack a single fox for the enjoyment of other people .
The fox stands no chance , so why is fox hunting legal whereas all other blood sports are banned .

But when it comes to ceasing the hunting and brutal killing of one of Britain 's few natural animals , they seem to turn a blind eye .
According to people who participate in fox hunting , it is an enjoyable sport .
A sport is a game in which two evenly matched teams or individuals partake for enjoyment or a prize .
It could be grossly unfair to match one footballer against a team of eleven , as the result would be a foregone conclusion .
If one boxer had to fight ten boxers , this would be unfair .
But matching one fox against a pack of dogs in a fight to the death is still considered sport .
Cricket is a sport that the brutal chase and killing of a fox for the enjoyment of the upper class is not .

Most of the infant educators , psychologists , and professionals in the education world think that using storytelling in early childhood education is good for their development .
But is it that good ?
Does storytelling have any disadvantages ?
Using storytelling is a good way to work on values and their emotions , as they are too young to express them by themselves . Using storytelling is a good way to work on values and emotions with them , as they are too young to express them by themselves . Alternatively and more accurately : Using storytelling is a good way to work on values and emotions with them , as they are too young to express themselves .
They see themselves in the main character , and through their experience they can learn how to act in these situations .
For instance , if the story is about fear , an emotion that makes them feel insecure , and ends up in a good way , they will have different methods to overcome their fear and feel more secure and self-confident .
Furthermore , they can take part and build up their own story .
Their vocabulary will increase at the same time they are working on their social abilities .
In addition , they can see that every act has consequences , and they have to be responsible .
However , there are some points that need to be considered .
Storytelling must be chosen according to the age of the pupils .
One of the reasons storytelling may not work is that some teachers expect more than their pupils can do .
Moreover , if the story is too long or dull , they will lose concentration easily and make their classmates lose it too .
To sum up , we must take advantage of storytelling to consolidate concepts , values , and emotions , and let imagination run wild .

The human brain is the most powerful computer known to man , yet it is small and light .
The brain is the control centre of the body , which can instruct it to move freely around its surroundings , and it is able to interact with other humans and objects .
The brain can make decisions ; it can communicate .
The only function of the brain that computers can rival is memory .
Some of the human brain 's functions have been taken over by computers , like accountancy , with the invention of electronic calculators .
In fact , the whole subject of mathematics has become quicker with the invention of the electronic calculator .
But the subject has not changed ; electronics have only solved a few mathematical puzzles .
Most of the theories used today were hypothesised and proved before the invention of the calculator .
Computers , however , have almost unimaginable accuracy .
Most high-precision engineering projects undertaken today use computers and laser technology to make parts accurate to thousandths of a millimeter .
The computer is very widely used in the modern day world , but in almost every case it is only an aid to the brain .
The human still has to tell the computer what to do .
Humans are still in charge .
The human brain is in no way made redundant by the invention of the computer , and I think that it will be a long time before technology discovers a way to make an electronic machine that will compete with the brain to achieve one of its functions , never mind all of them , which the human brain is capable of doing .

If the rate of car ownership continues to increase at such a rapid rate , then the roads will be completely congested .
This is the main problem facing the UK 's transport system .
The reasons for this are many and varied .
People today want more freedom and have more disposable income , both of which will lead to an increase in car ownership .
Many people also feel unsafe walking or using public transport to get to places , and mothers who would have walked to school when they were young insist on ferrying their children to school by car , as they believe , correctly or not , that there are too many child abductors around for it to be safe for children on the streets .
These views are supported by cases like the James Bulger case and the Fred and Mary West case , which have had very high publicity and have increased public awareness among people on the streets today .
People also use cars because they are more convenient than public transport as they can travel whenever they wish , and can travel door-to-door instead of having to walk to bus stops and stations .
The enormous levels of vehicles on the roads have meant that using a bicycle to travel has become unacceptable to many people , due to the danger and also to the levels of pollution from cars on the streets .
Rail travel has seen decreased popularity in recent years , due to the immense popularity of cars nowadays .
Some people may not use trains due to their seemingly unreliable service .
Trains also fail to offer the freedom of choice available with cars , as the passengers are tied to the timetables and locations of railway stations .
I think that the government should help Britain 's transport by aiming to decrease the amount of car usage and increase the usage of buses , trains and other forms of public transport .
The government should do this by investing more money in public transport than in road improvements , such as the widening of motorways .
This increased investment would lead to more attractive public transport , with more services on the timetables , lower fares and fewer delays .
These factors may make people switch from using their car to traveling to work or school and using buses or trains instead .
This would lead to less congested roads , which could then be used more efficiently by people with no other option , and a less polluted environment for all of us to live in .
This is because public transport is less polluting than personal car usage .
Scientists believe that it may not be safe to eat beef products .
Several years ago , the disease BSE , or 'Mad Cow Disease , ' became quite commonplace among cattle .
The disease incurs a mental deficiency , where the cow can not think for itself , and slowly dies .
This BSE has been known to cross the animal barriers ; several sheep have had a similar disease after eating feed made from the reminants of dead , meatstripped cows .
Now , scientists fear that it has crossed the boundary between cows and humans , as there are more and more cases of Creutzfeldt-Jakob Disease ( CJD ) appearing more frequently .
There is , as of yet , no cure for this disease , and the only way humans can contract it would be by eating beef products .
This clearly has put a lot of people off beef , as the press also had coverage of the inefficient quality control by the government , and the fact that this has been going on for years is worrying . However , a slightly more polished version could be : This clearly has put a lot of people off beef , as the press also covered the inefficient quality control by the government , and the fact that this has been going on for years is worrying . Corrected sentence : This clearly has put a lot of people off beef , as the press also covered the inefficient quality control by the government , and the fact that this has been going on for years is worrying .
The disease can take up to 15 - 20 years to become evident in humans , so even if people gave up beef today , they will still have a chance of getting CJD .
However , giving up the products now would reduce the chances of being crippled by this disease in the future .
If a lot of people did give up beef products , this would have had effects on the agricultural industry .
Cattle farmers will be hit particularly badly if no one wants to buy their meat .
It will affect other animals being sold for meat also ; more people will want to buy meat from sheep and pigs and so on , so they can still eat the same amount of meat .
The whole episode may send the price of beef down , so people will buy it and take the risk , which must be tiny , rather than forking out for more expensive meat products .
If no one wants to eat beef , then cows will only be bred for their milk , which means there will possibly be fewer cows in the future .
If cows are no longer required by the public for food , some abattoir workers may lose their jobs , and several butchers , for whom the money from beef products is a considerable percentage of their income , may be hit hard by this .
The politicians still say it is safe , and that they will continue to eat beef .
However , a lot of these people are old , and by the time the disease has developed in them , it wo n't really be too much of a premature death .
However , is the risk too great for us young people ?
I have n't stopped eating it .

The 20th Century invention that has had one of the most radical effects on people 's lives is the television .
During the 1950s , America witnessed the beginnings of a cultural revolution .
The era of Populuxe instigated a 'must-have ' ideology in the nation and the most important 'must-have ' was , of course , the television .
The presence of television has brought about several crucial trends in our culture : the mass culturization of various groups , the commercialization of our lifestyles , and the rapidity and breadth of the information that reaches us .
Gathered around the TV , the American family learned the 'ideal ' way of life .
But the picture of perfection was the same in every home .
We all received the same information .
We all saw the same families , the Cleavers and the Andersons , etc. , telling us how we should behave .
Mother was always beautiful , fathers knew best , and children had cute , silly , harmless problems .
As a result of this omniscient picture , a farmer in Iowa had an idea of what a family in New York consisted of . However , after re-examining , I found a slight possible improvement for better clarity and grammar : A more natural way to phrase it would be : As a result of this omniscient picture , a farmer in Iowa had an idea of what a typical family in New York consisted of . But since that is not drastically changing and it can be argued that ' a ' implies 'an example ' I will leave as As a result of this omniscient picture , a farmer in Iowa had an idea of what a family in New York consisted of .
People in N.Y. watched " Green Acres . "
Today , the same trend continues .
To white people , ghetto life is slightly less of a mystery .
The examples on television are blown up and exaggerated , but people get a general idea of different lifestyles .
Rather than having several small , isolated cultures , the United States is moving towards mass culturalization .
and the presence of another 's reality in our homes is a major part of the reason
Another effect of television on people 's lives is the commercialization of our lives .
Advertisements , which originally served only to inform people of their purchasing options , have developed into an art form .
15-second blocks of our time are sold for millions of dollars , and as a result , the American population is made to laugh , or to cry , and often to buy a product .
Finally , and perhaps most importantly , the citizens of America have experienced with the advent of the television a great increase in the amount of information they receive , as well as in the time it takes for it to reach them .
A hundred years ago , different sections of the country ( and the world ) were isolated and separated by the time it took to mail a letter and print a newspaper story .
Today , we know within seconds , or , in the case of the space shuttle Challenger explosion , we know it live , immediately .
This abundance of information has led to a drastic alteration in people 's ability to react to major events .
Our view of the world is different ; it 's closer ; it 's in our living rooms .
A good example of this is the reaction to the Vietnam War .
The war was , indeed , unpopular with or without television .
But the reality of what we saw , the casualty counts , the bloody children under the American flag , did much to enhance the negative aspects of war . should be But the reality of what we saw , the casualty counts , and the bloody children under the American flag , did much to enhance the negative aspects of war . becomes But the reality of what we saw , the casualty counts , and the images of bloody children under the American flag , did much to highlight the negative aspects of war . corrects to But the reality of what we saw , the casualty counts , and images of bloody children under the American flag , did much to highlight the negative aspects of war . final But the reality of what we saw , the casualty counts , and images of bloody children under the American flag , did much to highlight the negative aspects of war . becomes But the reality of what we saw , the casualty counts , and images of bloody children under the American flag , highlighted the negative aspects of war . Overall , the television has caused a radical change in our lives .
We are open to manipulation as well as to stimulation .
The television is a powerful and dangerous tool .
It can greatly enhance and improve our lives , but it is most important to be aware of the fact that it can be a manipulator .
We must be careful about what we watch .

My teaching philosophy changed considerably when I finished this course that was based on theories in second language acquisition .
Until now , my beliefs in teaching English have focused on the following opinions : ( i ) children should be familiar with English as early as possible , ( ii ) the teacher should give students motivation so that they can reach their target goal in learning a language , ( iii ) the teacher must be a good monitor in class , and ( iv ) the teacher must interact well with students .
My beliefs help me feel more confident about becoming an English teacher in the future .
First of all , parents should let their children learn English at an early age .
My first misunderstanding is that adults will acquire a second language better than children .
By reading child language acquisition in SLA , I know that the period during which people can acquire a second language best is in childhood ( McLaugh , 1978a , as cited in Gass and Selinker , 2008 , p.123 ) .
Moreover , children at the age of between 5 and 9 , which is called the critical period , can acquire a second language naturally and do not need any special methods of teaching .
Children have better phonology than adults and they display morphological sensitivity that adults can not .
However , older learners can be successful in second language ( L2 ) syntax .
Patkomski ( 1980 ) found that learners who learned L2 after the age of puberty received lower proficiency scores than those who started learning L2 before puberty .
Therefore , in the future , I will encourage everyone to let their child make an acquaintance with English as early as possible to help their children have an accent like native speakers .
If I have a chance to teach children , I will create an active atmosphere with various activities that focus on communication skills and give students opportunities to be exposed to authentic input such as cartoons , music , etc .
Secondly , the teacher should inspire students ' motivation and raise their awareness in learning so that they can achieve their target goal in language learning . When I was in grade ten , I did not have the motivation to learn English due to my parents ' obligation .
Consequently , my results did not meet the goal that my parents had expected .
Until I met a tutor invited by my parents , I passed the exam in class with a high mark , and I had motivation to learn better .
I want to become an English teacher .
Motivation is the second most important factor in SLA that makes students succeed in learning L2 ( Skehan , 1989 , as cited in Gass and Selinker , 2008 , p. 426 ) .
Students can use their whole time to do what they are interested in , and they will never get bored because of it . or Students can use their whole time to do what they are interested in , so they will never get bored .
The more motivated one has been in language learning , the more successful students will be .
It is really a long-term project that students can improve their proficiency in a second language .
They need to observe a number of comprehensible inputs and do many tasks to obtain their goal .
As a teacher , I will make efforts to increase the students ' frequency of motivation because of its changes over time , as detailed in Dörnyei and Ottó ( 1998 ) and in Dörnyei ( 2000 , 2001a ) , as cited in Gass and Selinker ( 2008 , p.428 ) .
Thirdly , the good teacher is the one that can organize all the activities in class well .
For instance , when I teach grammar , I have to define how many structures that I can teach in a lesson are enough , and with some difficult grammar rules , I need to break them down to teach in turn .
Learners need time to memorize the new rule and acquire it in their learned system .
After teaching the rule , I will ask my students to work in pairs and communicate using the new structure based on my cue cards .
When they are working , I can hear their conversation and know not only what they say but also how they say it , so I can tell whether they have acquired the rules or are just using their learned knowledge .
Finally , interaction is also an interesting theory .
Gass ( 2003 ) found that " language learning is stimulated by the communication of pressure and the relationship between communication and acquisition and the mechanisms . " becomes Gass ( 2003 ) found that " language learning is stimulated by the communication of pressure and the relationship between communication , acquisition , and the mechanisms . "
Therefore , I will teach my students in English only . I will let them have more chances to communicate with one another through the tasks that I give them in class . Then , I will move around the classroom and correct their mistakes through negotiation , recasts , or feedback .
When observing their dialogue , if they make mistakes , I will take note and after they finish their practice , I will correct them .
I advise interrupting their speech because it is unrespected them .
In addition , if I always correct mistakes , my students will lose their confidence and they will not like to practice anymore .
This is my philosophy on teaching foreign languages .
These beliefs help me examine what I am going to do in the future when I become an English teacher .
This course widened my knowledge a lot through the theories in the SLA book .
I think that students in a school of foreign language education must learn this course to have a better philosophy of teaching .
