European nations have over time been linked together both in war and in peace .
These countries have since been moving closer together along more institutional lines .
One such demonstration of this has been the formation of the European Community , made up of the European Coal and Steel Community , the European Atomic Energy Community , and the European Economic Community .
In 1987 , the European Community adopted the Single European Act , in which the member countries committed themselves to the realisation of a single internal European market by 1992 .
This act has raised questions in Britain as to whether it will result in a loss of sovereignty for Britain .
The lifting of trade barriers between the member states will enable the free movement of goods .
This economic union will not really create a loss of sovereignty for Britain , as it will merely facilitate the exchange of goods throughout Europe .
However , the fear is that the act will lead to decisions being imposed on Britain since an important element of it is the commitment to majority rule rather than the previously common practice of consensus decision-making in the Council of Ministers .
This would result in the ability of individual nations to veto key decisions being restricted . ( This sentence seems mostly correct but a bit wordy and awkward ; a more natural way to phrase it would be ) This would result in restricting the ability of individual nations to veto key decisions .
British sovereignty could be in danger if this union led to a European government imposing its authority on Britain . ( No changes needed , but I 'll make sure ) British sovereignty could be in danger if this union led to a European government imposing its authority over Britain .
A centralised European government would inhibit Britain 's decision-making ability .
The recent incident of the European Parliament imposing its ideals on Britain points out the authoritative principles to which it may be forced to accept if such a strong central body is created .
It is believed that Britain ought to halt construction on the Channel Tunnel link due to environmental concerns ; however , this action seemed to be an imposition on Britain 's sovereignty , as an external body was trying to tell the country what to do .
If the European Community were to bring in a single currency , Britain may be deprived of its sovereignty since it would lose its individuality , but more importantly , it would forget its bargaining position in the foreign exchange .
Currency decisions would be made by a central body , which Britain would have to accept .
If a single Europe should lead to British troops fighting on behalf of Europe instead of their own nation , most sovereignty would be lost .
It would mean a supranational force fighting as a whole , with no real difference between them - it would not be a case of " one nation , one force " .
However , the state would still exist as an island and people will always feel that they are British due to their roots and history .
Even if linked physically to Europe via the Channel Tunnel , Britain would still see itself as a separate country .
I personally believe that Britain will not lose its sovereignty if the union is based on an economic level of free trade between nations . However , a slight adjustment can make it more idiomatic and clear : I personally believe that Britain will not lose its sovereignty if the union is based on a free trade agreement at the economic level between nations . But given the original sentence is understandable and not incorrect in a major way , here is a minimally adjusted version : I personally believe that Britain will not lose its sovereignty if the union is based on free trade between nations at an economic level .
However , if a strong European government was created which made important decisions for Britain , such as currency settlements and the running of its foreign policy , this would mean that Britain would no longer be an independent state with the power to make its own decisions , and would hence lose its sovereignty .

Everyone is afraid of something , but a lot of people are more afraid of catastrophic events than of things like cancer .
Even though people are scared of these things , they continue to smoke and drink alcohol .
Some of our fears are instinctive , so we automatically respond to danger before we have even had time to think about it .
Fear makes us act instinctively ; we react so quickly that we save ourselves .
This type of fear is a necessary and life-saving response .
There are different kinds of fear , for example , phobias .
We experience phobias in situations that are not dangerous for our safety .
Many people have phobias , but they do not threaten their lives every day .
Scientists say that phobias arise from negative experiences or traumas and that they are difficult to control , but that they could be prevented with the right therapy .
We know what fear is thanks to experience and culture .
We were born with small and basic fears , but we know that things like terrorism are dangerous . Stories on TV , the internet , and newspapers increase the risk perception of extraordinary events and often influence our fears , leading us to worry about things that will never happen to us .
To better enjoy our lives without being oppressed by our fears , we must be objective as we watch programs on TV and pay more attention to what happens around us .

The continual development of computer technology has created a great deal of controversy in modern times . becomes The continuous development of computer technology has created a great deal of controversy in modern times .
There are nowadays widespread uses for computers in all parts of society .
One area that has drawn particular criticism is the computer games industry .
Since the early 1980s , when computers such as the Spectrum 48K and the Commodore 64 were introduced into the homes of millions of people , controversy has followed about their effect on children .
There is a widespread belief among parents that computer games hinder a child 's ability to learn .
The development of more sophisticated and technologically advanced computers , such as the Amiga and the PC , has served to deepen the problem .
The growing realism of the games appeals strongly to children .
However , parents feel that children should be broadening their minds by reading books and that the computer games industry is encouraging children not to learn . should be However , parents feel that children should broaden their minds by reading books and that the computer games industry is encouraging children not to learn .
Computers have also been blamed for a fall in education standards among primary school children ; a belief accentuated by the results of surveys which state that the vast majority of primary school children are unable to do simple arithmetic in their minds and rely on another computer , the calculator , to help them .
Another moral dilemma that computers have created is their role in the workplace .
There are many people who fear that computers will eventually replace people in the workplace .
The role of computers is already significant in employment areas , such as accountancy , which require a specialist ability to calculate and manipulate numbers .
These computers have replaced humans , and such changes have sparked fears that the level of unemployment could vastly increase as a result .
As computers are more efficient than humans , do not require payment for their work , are less temperamental than humans , and will never have a day off because they are ill , it seems that mankind is faced with a great problem .
Another claim made that suggests the human brain could become useless is that computers promote anti-social behaviour .
The creation of the World Wide Web and the Internet has created concern that the human race will become unsociable .
The Internet allows you to correspond with people all over the world , and it also contains many other functions that , supposedly , make life easier for us .
The Internet also has another fundamental problem , according to many .
The belief exists that the computer age and its developments , such as the Internet , will remove the challenges of life .
The human brain is constantly in need of being challenged to maintain itself ; however , with the introduction of the Internet , one could conduct their life without ever needing to leave the house , which many believe would menace society .
However , at the moment , the existence of computers is very much dependent on the presence of humans .
No matter how much artificial intelligence a computer may be able to show , it still has to rely on the human brain to program it and to put it into operation .
Although there are plans to create computers which can program themselves , ( which I personally feel is a very dangerous idea ) , the human brain still very much controls the computer and still has the ability to end the existence of computers at any given moment ; thankfully , a power computers do not have over humans .

Krashen 's theory is one of the most well-known and influential acquisition theories from the seventies .
Krashen presented this theory over several years in his works .
It was clustered in his great work : " The Input Hypothesis : Issues and Implications " ( 1985 ) , and it can be summarized in the next hypothesis :
• The acquisition-learning hypothesis .
• The Monitor hypothesis ,
• the Natural Order hypothesis
the Input Hypothesis
The Affective Filter hypothesis .
The Acquisition-Learning hypothesis is perhaps the most fundamental of all the hypotheses to be presented here .
It states that adults have two distinct and independent ways of developing competence in a second language .
On one hand , we have the acquisition that , according to Krashen , is the unconscious process children have from birth to develop their ability in their first language .
Language acquirers are not usually aware of the fact that they are acquiring that language .
They are not aware of the rules , they speak without thinking about what they are saying , and they do not stop to think about the errors they commit because they do not think they are doing anything wrong .
Some things " sound " good , and others do not .
On the other hand , we have the learning process ; it implies the development of competence in the second language .
We use the term " learning " to refer to the conscious knowledge we have of the second language , being aware of the rules , for example .
Some theorists say that children acquire language , but adults can not do it ; they just learn .
But according to Krashen , the acquisition-learning process suggests that adults can also acquire the ability to pick up languages , which does not disappear when we grow up .
But at the same time , it does not mean that adults can always achieve native language levels , or that they can have access to the same natural " language acquisition device " that children use ; it is so different .
Acquisition is a powerful process in adults . ( No changes needed , but I 'll provide a slightly rephrased version for better clarity , although not required ) Acquisition is a powerful process for adults .
Acquisition can not be converted into learning and vice versa .
They are two different processes ; acquisition is the most important one , because we have to control our mother language first , and after that , the learning of more languages .
An application for teaching , according to this theory , could be that the optimal way a language is learned is through natural communication .
As a second language teacher , the best thing is to create a situation where language is used in order to fulfil authentic purposes .
This will help students , children or adults , acquire the language instead of learning it .

The main problem in the United Kingdom is BSE , or as it is so-called , " Mad Cow Disease " .
It has been discovered that the disease can be transmitted to humans through the consumption of infected beef .
Beef production is a fairly large business in the U.K. , and it was necessary to discover more about this relatively new disease .
It was discovered that British farmers were to blame , due to their various industrial farming techniques .
The disease was originally carried by chickens .
When the farmers killed the chickens for their meat , the remains ( bone and organs ) were processed to provide a cheep feeding product .
Unfortunately the disease carrying organs were not just fed back to chickens but to cows as well .
The cows contracted the disease ( in a slightly different form ) and this was when " BSE " first emerged .
The correct thing to do would have been to destroy the infected cows , bringing an end to a potentially life-threatening situation .
However , the farmers had no money involved .
When the infected cows were slaughtered for beef , their remains were processed and fed back to other cattle spreading the disease further .
Unfortunately , unlike the chickens , the cattle were able to pass this disease to humans through their beef .
The same industrial techniques are still used today , and with the people in the UK becoming aware of the facts and more health conscious , the sales of beef have decreased .
It is impossible to know that you have contracted the disease for up to seven years .
And so , some attitudes of the public are : " Why should I stop eating beef if I could already have BSE ? "
Another public attitude is to ignore warnings as there have been no victims .
But it seems that the most popular option is to play it safe and quit beef entirely .
It seems that more and more families have opted for chicken , pork , or lamb as an alternative .
It could have devastating effects on the agricultural industry as well .
If there is a point where supply outweighs demand , farmers will produce less beef and earn less money .
It is therefore conceivable to think that farmers will switch from beef to an alternative product .

Many people are concerned about the increase in productive waste , garbage on the streets , and the lack of effective processing .
Nowadays , we still use traditional ways of recycling and rubbish gathering .

We collect our waste in one bag and then throw it into the special containers which are placed in each city area .
From time to time , approximately twice a week , this rubbish is unloaded into vehicles and taken away to a recycling site .
It is difficult to imagine further processing , but we know exactly that plastic and rubber waste is recycled .

Shaking stopped and the long , monotonous sound confirmed that Anna had just left this world for a better place .

Introduction to a paper
Supply chain involves the management and information provision for many areas in a company . It encompasses the selection of raw materials , the processing of raw materials into finished goods , and the transportation of those finished goods or products to the end customers .
The main parts are the suppliers , production , and distribution .
One important task is to provide the information in each area in order to create a logical connection between these main parts to approach the objective of selling a good quality product with a reduction in costs and time .
The definition of a standardized process is the establishment of the same method to be applied in the production of certain activities or functions .
This method is already accepted with the required parameters .
A standardized product is the result of a standardized process .
For example , the production of a Coca-Cola bottle in Brazil has to be the same as the production of a Coca-Cola bottle in Australia .
A standardized product must not have big deviations , in order to sell the same product to all customers .
Transport essentially constitutes our movements .
Cars ca n't always be afforded by all sections of society .
Public transport should be optimally run in accordance with demand .
Public spending should be spent appropriately to ensure the maximum benefit to the public .
Drive down any street in urban America and you will see young males and females , both black and white , driving Pathfinders , BMWs , Mercedes , and other luxury automobiles .
How do these young people acquire the funds to afford such expensive rides ?
They dress in Karl Kani , Pele Pele , and Guess clothing .
They wear Cartier wristwatches and expensive Nike shoes .
Where do the funds come from to purchase these fashion items ?
In many cases , the answer is simple : crime .
As unfortunate as it may sound , many youths are well aware of the fact that crime pays , and it pays well .
What alternatives does an inner-city youth have when faced with inescapable poverty ?
The answer becomes apparent when he or she is often surrounded by criminals living larger than those who take a more " conservative " path to financial security .
The philosophy is simple : if you want it , go get it — at any cost .
The consequences are minimal , especially when one considers the shockingly low percentage of criminals who actually end up in jail .
The only danger that exists for a criminal comes from other criminals trying to take what 's theirs .
Police are no threat as they are far outnumbered ; it is virtually a game of chance as to whether one gets caught in an act of crime .
Fortunately for the criminals , these odds are drastically in their favor . The public calls for more police but refuse to pay the taxes needed to hire them . Corrected sentence : Fortunately for the criminals , these odds are drastically in their favor . The public calls for more police but refuses to pay the taxes needed to hire them .
The few police on the street are thus often left chasing criminals , like a dog chasing its tail .
If a criminal is apprehended , and in an odd circumstance is placed in jail for a non-violent crime , it is only a matter of time ( often a short amount of time ) before he or she is free to return to the wealthy and comfortable living supported by burglary , mugging , dealing , or simple con games .
Jail space is reserved for murderers and rapists first , as it should be , and when a murderer is convicted and sentenced , a dealer is put back on the street .
What an ordinary citizen imagines when he or she witnesses or hears about a non-violent crime is a thug bent on destroying society : killing babies , smoking as much weed as he or she can get their hands on , etc .
In reality , these criminals are merely working a job that pays them better than any other job .
Why work at McDonald 's where you are forced to work in a hot , cramped atmosphere , possibly with an overbearing boss who is stuck in a service job with no end in sight , making $ 5.00 an hour and shopping at K-Mart for clothes ?
It is obvious that crime does not pay .
The proof exists on any street in urban America : underprivileged youth rolling in luxury automobiles and stuffing wads of money into their designer jeans .
This is less of a choice than it is an act of taking advantage of an opportunity .
There are few alternatives for low-income youths , and even fewer obstacles in the quest for cash .
With violent crime rising and financial support for more police falling , criminals will continue to profit .

It is undeniable that housing and transport networks are very important for us , but plenty of people choose to build these in areas of moorland , forest , and wetland , which destroy the animals ' living areas and pollute the environment we live in .
In my opinion , it is time for governments to take action .
To begin with , the energy in the world is limited . In other words , what we eat and what we need depends on farming and forestry . If we run out of resources , building more large-scale buildings would ultimately lead to a disaster .
As for the animals , a series of large-scale construction projects are being built , and they can not live in the forest anymore , having to move to other places . According to the China Daily , it has reported that three elephants entered a town and ate crops . This is because their habitats were built into roads . Many kinds of animals have to change their living habits , adapting to what people have done .
For the sea species , many visiting boats are put into the sea , polluting the ocean , leading to a high death rate .
To solve these intractable problems , the governments need to take measures .
For example , education is the key to raising people 's responsibility ; governments can teach through public media . They can also allow organizations to go around the world and spread the problems that areas have destroyed . These may be long-term solutions , but they are more realistic solutions than setting up yet another international organization .
One of the greatest inventions of all time is a television .
The invention that swept the world and changed leisure habits for countless millions was pioneered by the Scottish-born electrical engineer John Logie Baird .
It had been realized for some time that light could be converted into electrical impulses , making it possible to transmit such impulses over a distance and then reconvert them into light .
And now it has become one of the most important mass media .
Millions of people all over the world like to watch TV in their spare time .
It informs , educates , and entertains them .
It influences the way people look at the world and makes them change their views .
TV simply helps us to relax after a hard day 's work , offering a great variety of entertaining and musical programs .
But there are some opinions that television does a lot of harm .
People are beginning to forget how to occupy their free time .
It prevents them from communicating with each other , visiting friends , or visiting relatives .
And indeed , people used to have hobbies , they used to go outside for amusement to the theatre , cinema , and sporting events .
They used to read books and listen to music .
Now all my free time is given to television .
Still , it 's not a good thing for children to be glued to the TV screen all day long .
It 's very harmful for their health and for the development of their personalities , because children prefer low-standard hits , horror films , or banal serials .
I 'm not much of a passionate TV viewer .
In fact , I only watch those programs that I find interesting and helpful .
I relax when I watch musical shows , humorous programs , and TV games .
To my mind , all these things depend on the lifestyle of people .
Nevertheless , television has obviously changed society , and it is probably used more than any other type of mass media .

The Cherepovets match factory " FESKO " is the leading company in the match branch of industry .
It is the largest manufacturer of matches in the post-Soviet space and in Europe .
At the same time , the company continues to grow , increasing production and strengthening its position in the market .
The first attempt to build the Cherepovetsk match factory was in 1948 , when construction of the factory on the banks of the river Yagorba began .
But a set of equipment for the match production was not received .
The building was developed into a plywood pipe plant .
The match factory was built only in 1970 seems mostly correct but a slight tweak could make it clearer . The match factory was built as recently as 1970 .
It was planned to buy equipment for production in Sweden , but eventually the factory was equipped with domestic precision equipment .
Then the Cherepovetsk factory 's capacity was almost the worst in the industry .
General reconstruction of the company began in 1981 .
Five " Arenko " automatic production lines were mounted over three years , and at the end of the technology modernization , 70 % of the equipment had been replaced with brand-new ones .
And it was the beginning of an ascent into a leading position in the industry .
Since 2012 , " FESKO " has been carrying out a large-scale modernization , which cost more than 200 million rubles .

Nowadays , more and more people tend to have a healthy lifestyle .
Everybody wants to be healthy and to visit their doctor only once per year for a health evaluation .
However , living a healthy lifestyle is not easy ; it requires following the next steps , such as : eating a healthy diet , exercising regularly , and getting enough sleep at night .
Physical activity is one of the most important aspects of a healthy lifestyle .
Regular exercise not only keeps your body physically strong , but also reduces the likelihood of getting many health-related problems and increases tolerance to stressful situations .
It is a fact that physical exercise makes our skeletal-muscle system stronger .
Well-developed and strong vertebral muscles keep our body in the right vertical position , so vertebral deformation will not develop and back pain will not occur .
Indeed , doing a special type of gym activity called " cardio " improves blood circulation in internal organs and the heart .
Accordingly , the risk of cardiovascular diseases decreases .
Also , everybody knows that strong positive or negative emotions , due to certain hormonal reactions , have an impact on the heart 's work .
In a regular person , heart rate and blood pressure can increase dramatically and even cause a stroke or a heart attack .
In trained people , the intention of heart contractions and stroke volume will increase .
The heart rate will change slightly .
Thus , trained people have better tolerance for stressful situations .
Food that we consume is the next issue of a healthy lifestyle .
A healthy diet consists of balanced , fresh , and unprocessed food with a proper amount of calories .
Our daily food should include enough protein , carbohydrates , fat , minerals , and vitamins , which are required for normal body functions .
For instance , a lack of protein causes muscle weakness ; a lack of vitamin A causes myopia and night blindness .
Also , if food is not fresh or not prepared properly , it can contain bacteria or parasites .
For example , spoiled milk products can lead to gastro-intestinal tract dysfunctions , and not properly thermal processing seafood can cause leptospirosis .
Moreover , fast food should not be on the table .
Avoiding eating fast-food products , we diminish a risk factor for getting some serious diseases , such as cancer .
French fries are just one example .
Fries are usually cooked in a large amount of oil which boils all day .
According to science , in addition , we have to limit the size of portions and consume only an amount of calories according to our individual needs .
In this way , we will never have problems with obesity .
Being healthy is fun !
You may think being unhealthy is only about being fat , but that 's not true .
Being unhealthy leads to multiple diseases , such as heart or breathing problems , and even depression .
Besides this being very awful , staying healthy is a good way to feel good about yourself , find new interests and make new friends .
Here are some suggestions for you who want to be healthy :
Instead of going to a fast food chain during your lunchtime , why do n't you try going to our cafeteria on campus , which has a wide variety of salads and soups that are not only healthy but also really tasty ?
Did you know that our athletics team is accepting registrations ?
This could be a great way to find new teammates who would help you develop some skills .
Do n't waste time , run to get the last spots .
Right outside our campus , you can find a gym that offers a lot of activities , such as spinning , aerobics , or even swimming lessons .
Also , because you are studying in this college , they will give you a big discount !

The name of the film is " Bangalore Days . "

This type of surgery has a low mortality risk because of the low likelihood of human error .
Although the operation was successful and my mother was healthy again .
The doctor had to remove her ovaries during the surgery after he accidentally caused a hemorrhage in them .
He made a human mistake and my mother barely survived her liver operation with the unannounced removal of her ovaries .
The overwhelming panic that I felt during her operation and the pain we went through as a family after her surgery has changed the shape of my life forever .
Due to a human mistake , neither my life nor my mother 's life was ever the same again .
Ever since that day , I have wanted to be an engineer to design a robotic system that can perform surgeries with high accuracy , thus eliminating the human error margin .
I studied mechatronics engineering with the hope that one day , with enough knowledge and willpower , I would be able to work and contribute to the field of engineering .
I am both hardworking and resilient .

The computer has been a major technological invention of great importance .
We are able to perform tasks such as writing letters at the push of a button , use programs , and even play games with these masterpieces .
A person of any age can use a computer for business or pleasure , and generally , the machine is a superb enhancement in our ever-expanding , business-orientated world .
With health experts , however , our marvellous machine provokes health problems that must not be ignored .
Apart from being a necessity for some , it makes human beings lazy to a certain extent and thus , allows us to use our brains less and less .
It is true to say that a computer is able to perform many hundreds of useful tasks to which our brains are completely indifferent .
But we ought to ask ourselves " What happens when the computer-orientated world collapses ? "
We would then have to use our brains .
It is not sensible to put all our efforts and hopes into a machine that runs on electricity .
The brain must be exercised to allow for this possible danger , if we are disconnected from our precious computers .
We must educate ourselves more and our children especially , who are at the forefront of tomorrow 's technology .

It is killing the planet .
Our love of convenience will cause the end of our beautiful planet and , of course , us as well .
In most large cities around the world , cars are actually inconvenient nowadays , and most people rely on public transport to get around .
The Paris Metro , New York Subway and London Underground are all an integral part of these thriving cities .
In many cities , there are not only massive traffic jams , but there is nowhere to park your car once you get to your destination .
If there is to be a public , they will need to use and enjoy public transportation .
The model does need some work , however , such as smaller and more frequent buses during most of the day , with the big buses only coming out during rush hours .
The future is all about public transport , with the private gas-driven car a thing of the past .
If we make it past this disaster , we will be saying " What were we thinking ? " .

This line graph shows the number of visitors to a selection of some different museums and galleries in Sharjah . Overall , the greatest number of visitors was in Sharjah Museum of Islamic Civilisation and the least number of visitors was for Maraya Art Centre .
The most noticeable aspect of the data in the Sharjah Art Museum is that it started in 1991 and increased slightly until 2001 , then it rose sharply to reach a peak of approximately 3.2 in 2006 . Secondly , if we look at the Sharjah Calligraphy Museum and the Sharjah Archeology Museum , we can notice that both lines started in the same year , 1991 . The Archeology Museum started with a number of 0.3 , then it remained steady until 2001 , after which it increased sharply . The Calligraphy Museum started with 1 million visitors and decreased slightly until 1996 to reach 0.9 million visitors , then it remained stable until 2006 , after which it dropped to 0.5 million .

For instance , we have many examples to prove that public transport itself is improving our environment .
London 's subway , for example , carries more than one thousand people every day .
People barely use their cars in crowded cities ; that is why public transport still has a unique role in our daily lives .

The recent developments in the field of genetic engineering have come largely as a result of discoveries made and techniques designed during this century , starting with the discovery of DNA and the mapping and understanding of its structure .
The manipulation of genes is an incredibly important and dangerously powerful ability which can not be left simply to the scientists to look after .
We are all now affected by the results of genetic engineering , be it for medical reasons or commercial ones .
Tomatoes are designed and engineered to last longer , apples to grow bigger , crops to ripen later to allow for transport time , and pigs are used to grow insulin for human use .
The list is enormous .
Along with the many advantages , there are dangers .
New biological weapons are being developed all over the world ; for example , the ability to transfer the genes that cause cancer into a simple disease such as the common cold could , without much doubt , wipe out a significant percentage of the human race .
There need not be a war for something disastrous like this to occur ; these genetically engineered microbes could be released accidentally while being investigated in an unsealed laboratory .
If we are going to accept the advantages that come with genetic engineering , we also have to take responsibility for the disadvantages ; the stakes are too high to leave this job to the scientists , and they ca n't be expected to take the moral responsibility for people who misuse the discoveries or inventions , thereby causing disaster .
Governments should ensure that money is invested not only in the research of genetic engineering , but also in ensuring that the results of this research are kept safe .
I recommend visiting a Guido mine is not incorrect however it could be more accurate , A more accurate sentence would be I recommend visiting the Guido mine .
It 's an old mine , which was converted into a cultural zone in our city .
Of course , it 's still a mine , so you can see all the main mining equipment used - Zabrze is located in Silesia , an area with coal mines .
It was set up in 1855 by Guido Henckel von Donnersmarck , and so the mine was named .
It has such a rich history that I ca n't tell you everything in one e-mail .
I can say only that the mine is divided into two levels : 170 and 320 .
The first one , level 170 , presents methods of mining , the work of miners in the late 19th century , and the history of that industry in Silesia .
This level is made up of an interactive form of sightseeing supported by lights and sounds .
The main assumption is to shock the visitor and make him feel , and , in my opinion , it surely does .
The visitors may be surprised by the noise of crackling ceilings or rats ' squealing .
There are also many exhibitions organised throughout the year .
Highly qualified guides are waiting for every group of visitors and they are ready for even the most serious avalanche of questions .
On the path of sightseeing , you can also find a chapel - a place which is very important for every minor and , of course , a place where important celebrations take place .
On level 320 , which resembles a real mine , you can see a longwall coal-cutting machine while it 's working .
You can also touch real coal with your bare hands .
There are many organised concerts , exhibitions and theatre plays too .
And if you get hungry , you can try something regional - you may be sure that the cooks wo n't let you starve to death .
I think that the Guido Mine is well worth visiting .

Nowadays , the aeroplane is treated as an ordinary part of our life .
Its chief purpose is to transport people safely from one place to another .
However , a few decades ago , we had a very limited notion of such technology .
Yet , in the present , it is so ubiquitous that we seem not to take notice of air pollution .
If one were to delve into the most paramount inventions of the last century , they would probably identify modern conveniences , namely television or the computer .
We tend to underrate the importance of the aeroplane .
It is clear that air travel has had an enormous impact on the way we perceive the world .
Firstly , as a result of its development , we can experience a noticeable surge in mass tourism .
People have ample opportunities to set off on a riveting journey to places they previously imagined while reading an adventurous book . People have ample opportunities to set off on a riveting journey to places they had previously imagined while reading an adventurous book .
Besides , the great influence of the aeroplane may be seen in mass migration .
Had it not been for the Wright brothers , emigrants and casualties would not have been able to settle in remote lands ; hence , the world would teeter financially .
As far as the vast changes which the aeroplane has undergone are concerned , society 's attitude has also improved .
For decades , we had a distant relationship with such an initially fallible workhorse .
A classic illustration of this could be the use of air machines only for military purposes .
Since the 20th century was marked by wars , we only killed and exterminated people .
Additionally , creating such a vehicle had been our morbid fascination since time immemorial .
Nonetheless , the situation has somewhat normalized .
Air travel has changed from a luxury at the rich 's disposal to a common thing available to almost everyone .
I personally believe that the influence that the aeroplane has had on our lives is significant ; however , we have to bear in mind the dangers connected with it .
For instance , at the beginning of the 21st century , tourists have been under the constant threat of terrorists .
Moreover , the opportunities that air technology brings may easily contribute to further development .
Perhaps it will improve to such an extent that commuting from Tokyo to London would be in the twinkling of an eye .
To sum up , the air business and its changes have been important for the world .
Apart from minor drawbacks , we can only laud its benefits .
It has certainly had an edifying effect on our thinking about travelling .
Many years ago , people lived without all the things we have nowadays , such as mobile phones , LED TVs , computers , etc .
This means that we have experienced an important change with the passing of time . It is due to the rise of technology , and it entails that people 's lives change .
Now , will we continue to develop our technology and our lives ?
From my point of view , technology will continue changing our lives in aspects of routine and free time , to the point that we will not be able to live without using it .
There is a problem ; we must not depend on items like phones , TVs , and all items created by technology .
If we had to live in the past , bearing in mind all our dependency on technology , we would not be able to live in this way , I am sure of it .
Nonetheless , I think that people 's lives will improve thanks to technology . Not only does it refer to negative aspects , such as dependency on technology , but it also offers us interesting things , like new technologies and new information systems , in order to improve the world of work , the improvement in a wide range of job sectors , including agriculture , healthcare systems , etc .
Finally , to sum up , I think that people 's lives will change , but not dramatically ; it depends on each person and the way they focus their lives .
Unfortunately , I have n't seen any thrillers for ages .
I prefer other genres .
I saw a really great comedy directed by Wes Anderson last month .
The title is The Grand Budapest Hotel .
The story took place in Eastern Europe , between the two world wars .
The hotel manager used to take care of his regular clients , especially old ladies .
The hotel flourished and the manager felt powerful and behaved like a God in his small universe .
He hired the teenage Indian refugee as a bellboy and taught him all his skills .
He gave the boy a lot of lessons in hospitality , friendship , courage , and humanity .
An old man came back to the place of his youth and told a story about his friend and master .
Nowadays , public transport is less convenient than travelling by car because there are other solutions , like online platforms that allow sharing a car for a relatively low price with people who are going to the same destination .
Sharing the car could be an alternative to save money , but it is also more comfortable than traveling with a lot of people .
First of all , public transport has fewer combinations ; it is too difficult to travel , for example , if you have to work at night and on special days it is impossible to get a seat .
On the other hand , if you have missed the bus , train or any other public transport , you have to wait a long time for the next one and it can be maddening .
In conclusion , people prefer traveling by car because it is more comfortable , they can go everywhere they want at the hour they consider best and choose to share the space with other people or not .
Nowadays people spend lots of money in order to go to an English-speaking country to improve their language skills .
But is it really the most effective way to learn a language ?
From my point of view , studying in a foreign country has some drawbacks .
Firstly , this way is very expensive as the tuition fee for overseas students is quite high .
Besides , when you study abroad , you have to adapt to a very different way of life , which can be quite stressful .
What is more , English teachers do not speak Russian , so if you do n't know English well , you will not understand their explanations .
It is often assumed that it is better to study a language abroad because you can always use it when speaking with native speakers .
However , I doubt that we will have lots of opportunities to speak abroad since we do not know many people there .
It is also believed that Russian teachers are not as qualified as those in Britain .
I totally disagree with this opinion because Russian teachers can compare two languages and explain the grammar rules better .
To sum up , I would argue that the best way to learn a language is to study it in a foreign country because you can always get the necessary help from your teachers .
Moreover , today we have lots of opportunities to improve our skills , such as communicating with English pen friends over the Internet .
I think that we should travel abroad so as to practice a language but not to study it .
